<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id79911_739566-ca alignnone has-theme-palette9-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column79911_9f65c9-b2 inner-column-1"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h1 class="kt-adv-heading79911_aecfca-75 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79911_aecfca-75"><strong>Modern &amp; Mindful Quilting</strong></h1>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color has-medium-font-size">Taking time to enjoy the process of quilting. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color has-medium-font-size">Combine slow stitching, different techniques and modern designs to make quilts and accessories that can be used in everyday life.</p>



<div style="height:25px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>



<p class="has-text-align-center"> If you love patchwork and quilting &#8211; or are curious about it &#8211; I&#8217;m here to encourage you to pick up needle and thread!</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">My goal is to help everyone learn to stitch, to carve out time in their busy schedules and find their own stitchy style. </p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">I include a <strong><a href="https://fabricandflowers.co.uk/learn-quilting/">Learn to Quilt</a></strong> series for the beginner, <a href="https://shop.fabricandflowers.co.uk/"><strong>design patterns</strong></a> &amp; <a href="https://learn.fabricandflowers.co.uk/"><strong>courses</strong></a> and share techniques and tutorials here on my website.</p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Let’s get stitching!</p>



<div style="height:50px" aria-hidden="true" class="wp-block-spacer"></div>
</div></div>

</div></div>

<h5 class="kt-adv-heading79911_a506bf-fa wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading79911_a506bf-fa">Organise your quilting!</h5>
